  # 1ï¸âƒ£ **ğŸ¢ Office Buildings** (Corporate HQs, Multi-Tenant, Coworking)

  ## **ğŸ“Œ Overview**

  Office buildings, including **corporate headquarters, multi-tenant spaces, and coworking environments**, generate significant procurement activity related to **facility renovations, space planning, technology integration, and maintenance services**. Scan2Plan should focus on integrating with procurement platforms and vendor programs used by the largest real estate management firms and corporate tenants.  
    
  ---

  ## **1ï¸âƒ£ Key Procurement Drivers**

* **Corporate Facility Upgrades** â€“ Tenant improvements, sustainability initiatives, and office space reconfiguration.  
    
* **Workplace Technology** â€“ Digital twin modeling, 3D scanning, security upgrades.  
    
* **Asset Lifecycle Management** â€“ Ongoing maintenance contracts for HVAC, electrical, and structural upgrades.  
    
* **Coworking & Flexible Space Expansion** â€“ Rapid space repurposing in coworking hubs and corporate real estate portfolios.  
    
  ---

  ## **2ï¸âƒ£ Top Procurement Sources**

  ### **ğŸ¢ Corporate Real Estate Services & Facilities Management Firms**

  These firms manage large-scale office buildings and lease commercial space to corporate tenants.

| Company | Sector | Procurement Process |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| CBRE | Corporate, Multi-Tenant | Vendor registration is by **invitation only** through CBREâ€™s **mySupplier** platform. Contact a CBRE representative to inquire. [More Info](https://www.cbre.com/about-us/suppliers) |
| JLL | Commercial Real Estate | Vendors must undergo a due diligence process before onboarding. Initiate by contacting a JLL partner. [More Info](https://www.us.jll.com/en/about-jll/suppliers) |
| Cushman & Wakefield | Property Management | Potential suppliers can express interest through the **Prospective Supplier Registration Portal**. [Register Here](https://cushwake.supplierone.co/) |

| Colliers | Office Property Management | Vendor onboarding is handled regionally. Contact local procurement managers. [More Info](https://www.colliers.com/en) |

## **CBRE**

â€‹CBRE's procurement process is designed to ensure that suppliers meet their standards for quality, compliance, and sustainability. Here's a detailed overview:â€‹

### **1\. Supplier Engagement**

* **Invitation to Register**: Prospective suppliers are typically invited to register by a CBRE representative. This invitation initiates the onboarding process. â€‹

  ### **2\. Registration via mySupplier Portal**

* **Access**: Suppliers receive an email invitation to join the **mySupplier** portal, CBRE's platform for supplier onboarding and compliance management. â€‹[elbresources.ocgsoftware.com+4elbresources.ocgsoftware.com+4emerald.cbre.com+4](https://elbresources.ocgsoftware.com/mediaResources/cbre/application/pdf/17a86d833b65496130700a84f01b79eb4f3208444fb)  
    
* **Profile Creation**: Suppliers must create a user profile, providing detailed company information, including:â€‹  
    
  * Legal entity name and addressâ€‹[cbreexcellerate.com+2cbre-resources.cleverstory.io+2CBRE+2](https://cbre-resources.cleverstory.io/cbre)  
  * Tax identification numbersâ€‹[CBRE+1mysupplier.cbre.com+1](https://www.cbre.com/about-us/supply-chain/suppliers-supply-chain-technologies-and-registration)  
  * Banking detailsâ€‹[mysupplier.cbre.com+2elbresources.ocgsoftware.com+2CBRE+2](https://elbresources.ocgsoftware.com/mediaResources/cbre/application/pdf/1754ac8bd54ca154343b24f45e48a417cbad9d00a36)  
  * Certificates and licensesâ€‹


* *Note: The registration process is comprehensive and may take around one hour to complete.* â€‹[CBRE](https://www.cbre.com/about-us/supply-chain/mysupplier-training-portal)

  ### **3\. Compliance and Documentation**

* **Document Submission**: Suppliers are required to upload relevant documents, such as insurance certificates and compliance certifications.â€‹  
    
* **Risk Assessment**: CBRE conducts a risk assessment to evaluate the supplier's compliance with legal and regulatory standards. This may involve third-party reviews and can take up to 60 days. â€‹[mediaassets.cbre.com](https://mediaassets.cbre.com/-/media/project/cbre/dotcom/global/about/suppliers/supplier-shield/training-guides/understanding-and-completing-the-risk-access-process.pdf?rev=7b13f25206904d57886141bb96f29a68)

  ### **4\. Approval and Onboarding**

* **Profile Review**: Once all information is submitted, CBRE's procurement team reviews the supplier's profile.â€‹  
    
* **Approval Notification**: Approved suppliers receive confirmation and are added to CBRE's supplier database, making them eligible for procurement opportunities.â€‹

  ### **5\. Performance Monitoring**

* **Ongoing Evaluation**: CBRE monitors supplier performance to ensure adherence to contractual obligations and quality standards.â€‹  
    
  By following this structured process, CBRE ensures that its suppliers align with the company's commitment to excellence and compliance.

  ## **JLL**

  â€‹Jones Lang LaSalle (JLL) has established a comprehensive procurement process to ensure that suppliers meet their standards for quality, compliance, and sustainability. Here's a detailed breakdown:â€‹

  ### **1\. Supplier Engagement**

* **Invitation to Register**: Prospective suppliers are typically invited by a JLL representative to participate in the procurement process. This invitation initiates the onboarding procedure. â€‹[us.jll.com](https://www.us.jll.com/en/vendors-suppliers)

  ### **2\. Registration and Pre-Qualification**

* **Online Registration**: Suppliers are required to register through JLL's e-procurement portal, managed by illion TenderLink. This portal is used to advertise tenders and manage the procurement process through to contract award. Registration is free of charge. â€‹[portal.tenderlink.com+3tenderlink.com+3portal.tenderlink.com+3](https://www.tenderlink.com/jll/)  
    
* **Pre-Qualification Form (PQF)**: After registration, suppliers must complete a Pre-Qualification Form, providing detailed information about their company, services, and compliance with JLL's standards. â€‹[pages.avetta.com+1pages.avetta.com+1](https://pages.avetta.com/rs/752-BVH-753/images/JLL%20Supplier%20Portal%20Request_Intel.pdf)

  ### **3\. Compliance and Documentation**

* **Document Submission**: Suppliers are required to submit necessary documentation, which may include:â€‹  
    
  * Non-Disclosure Agreementsâ€‹[us.jll.com](https://www.us.jll.com/en/vendors-suppliers)  
  * Certificates of Insuranceâ€‹[pages.picsauditing.com+4us.jll.com+4pages.avetta.com+4](https://www.us.jll.com/en/vendors-suppliers)  
  * Risk Assessment Profilesâ€‹[us.jll.com](https://www.us.jll.com/en/vendors-suppliers)  
  * Environmental Health and Safety (EHS) programsâ€‹


* These documents are collected to ensure compliance with JLL's corporate standards and regulatory requirements. â€‹[pages.avetta.com](https://pages.avetta.com/rs/752-BVH-753/images/JLL%20Supplier%20Portal%20Request_Intel.pdf)  
    
* **Third-Party Compliance Management**: JLL has partnered with Avetta (formerly PICS Auditing) to manage supplier compliance. Avetta validates supplier documentation and adherence to JLL and client standards, using a Red, Amber, Green flag status system. â€‹[pages.avetta.com+3pages.avetta.com+3pages.avetta.com+3](https://pages.avetta.com/rs/752-BVH-753/images/JLL%20Supplier%20Portal%20Request_Intel.pdf)

  ### **4\. Evaluation and Approval**

* **Assessment**: JLL's procurement team, along with Avetta, evaluates the submitted information to ensure compliance with JLL's standards. This includes reviewing safety records, financial health, and insurance coverage. â€‹[pages.avetta.com](https://pages.avetta.com/rs/752-BVH-753/images/JLL%20Supplier%20Portal%20Request_Intel.pdf)  
    
* **Approval Notification**: Once approved, suppliers receive confirmation and are added to JLL's supplier database, making them eligible for procurement opportunities.â€‹

  ### **5\. Performance Monitoring**

* **Ongoing Evaluation**: JLL regularly monitors supplier performance to ensure adherence to contractual obligations and quality standards. This ongoing assessment helps maintain high levels of service delivery.â€‹  
    
  By following this structured procurement process, JLL ensures that its suppliers align with the company's commitment to excellence, safety, and sustainability.

  ## **â€‹Cushman & Wakefield**

  â€‹Cushman & Wakefield has established a comprehensive procurement process to ensure that suppliers meet their standards for quality, compliance, and sustainability. Here's a detailed breakdown:â€‹

  ### **1\. Supplier Registration**

* **Prospective Supplier Registration Portal**: Suppliers interested in partnering with Cushman & Wakefield are encouraged to register through the **Prospective Supplier Registration Portal**. This portal allows suppliers to express interest in providing goods or services to the company and its clients. Registration is free of charge. â€‹[cushmanwakefield.supplierone.co+1Cushman & Wakefield+1](https://cushmanwakefield.supplierone.co/)  
    
  * **Registration Steps**:  
    1. Visit the [Prospective Supplier Registration Portal](https://cushmanwakefield.supplierone.co/).  
    2. Click on "Register" to create a new account.  
    3. Provide the necessary company information, including legal name, address, and contact details.  
    4. Submit the registration form for review.


* **E-Procurement Portal via TenderLink**: Cushman & Wakefield utilizes the TenderLink portal to release tenders and manage purchasing requirements. Suppliers must register on this platform to receive tender notifications and participate in procurement opportunities. Registration is free. â€‹[portal.tenderlink.com](https://portal.tenderlink.com/cushmanwakefield/login)  
    
  * **Registration Steps**:  
      
    1. Visit the [Cushman & Wakefield E-Procurement Portal](https://portal.tenderlink.com/cushmanwakefield/login).  
    2. Click on the "Registration" tab to begin the process.  
    3. Complete the required fields with accurate company information.  
    4. Agree to the terms of service and submit the registration.

    ### **2\. Compliance and Documentation**

* **Avetta Compliance Management**: To ensure a safe and sustainable workplace, Cushman & Wakefield has partnered with Avetta, a supplier prequalification and compliance management service. Suppliers are required to register with Avetta to maintain compliance and qualify for work with Cushman & Wakefield and C\&W Services. â€‹[pages.avetta.com+1pages.avetta.com+1](https://pages.avetta.com/Cushman-Wakefield.html)  
    
  * **Registration Steps**:  
      
    1. Visit the [Avetta Registration Page](https://pages.avetta.com/Cushman-Wakefield.html).  
    2. Follow the on-screen instructions to create an account and submit necessary compliance documentation.  
    3. Achieve and maintain a compliant status to be eligible for procurement opportunities.

    ### **3\. Evaluation and Approval**

* **Preferred Supplier Program**: Cushman & Wakefield's procurement platform strategically manages a set number of national supplier partners by category through their Preferred Supplier Program. This program focuses on offering clients and internal stakeholders the best services and goods at optimal value by leveraging significant spending across the company. â€‹[Cushman & Wakefield+1Cushman & Wakefield+1](https://www.cushmanwakefield.com/en/about-us/supplier-management/preferred-supplier-program)  
    
  * **Benefits**:  
      
    * Increased savings opportunities.  
    * Pre-negotiated terms and conditions to streamline the procurement process.  
    * Access to a network of suppliers committed to quality, innovation, responsiveness, and cost-effectiveness.

    ### **4\. Performance Monitoring**

* **Annual Reviews**: Each supplier in Cushman & Wakefield's network is reviewed annually to ensure strong operational practices, appropriate health and safety records, and adherence to industry standards. This ongoing evaluation helps maintain high levels of service delivery and compliance. â€‹[Cushman & Wakefield](https://www.cushmanwakefield.com/en/about-us/supplier-management)  
    
  By following this structured procurement process, Cushman & Wakefield ensures that its suppliers align with the company's commitment to excellence, safety, and sustainability.

  ## **ğŸ”‘ Colliers Vendor Prequalification Process**

  **1\. Complete the REMS Vendor Qualifier Form**  
    
  Colliers requires prospective vendors to fill out their Real Estate Management Services (REMS) Vendor Qualifier Form. This form assesses your company's capabilities and readiness to partner with Colliers on a national scale. Key areas covered include:â€‹[Colliers](https://www.colliers.com/en/services/real-estate-management-services/vendor-qualifier-form?utm_source=chatgpt.com)  
    
* **Service Scope**: Indicate if your services are available across all U.S. markets.â€‹  
    
* **Colliers Master Services Agreement**: Confirm your ability to sign this agreement.â€‹  
    
* **Single Point of Contact**: Provide a dedicated contact for Colliers.â€‹  
    
* **Spend Aggregation**: Demonstrate your ability to aggregate Colliers' total spend across offices.â€‹[Colliers+1Colliers+1](https://www.colliers.com/en/services/real-estate-management-services/vendor-qualifier-form?utm_source=chatgpt.com)  
    
* **Discounted Pricing**: Offer competitive pricing aligned with Colliers' national footprint.â€‹[Colliers](https://www.colliers.com/en/services/real-estate-management-services/vendor-qualifier-form?utm_source=chatgpt.com)  
    
* **Escalation Path**: Detail a customized escalation process for service issues.â€‹[Colliers+4Colliers+4Colliers+4](https://www.colliers.com/en/services/real-estate-management-services/vendor-qualifier-form?utm_source=chatgpt.com)  
    
* **Reciprocal Business**: Indicate willingness to introduce Colliers to decision-makers in your organization.â€‹  
    
* **ISO Compliance**: State your compliance with International Organization for Standardization standards.â€‹[Colliers+3Colliers+3Colliers+3](https://www.colliers.com/en/services/real-estate-management-services/vendor-qualifier-form?utm_source=chatgpt.com)  
    
  **Action**: Complete the form available here: [Colliers REMS Vendor Qualifier Form](https://www.colliers.com/en/services/real-estate-management-services/vendor-qualifier-form).â€‹[Colliers](https://www.colliers.com/en/services/real-estate-management-services/vendor-qualifier-form?utm_source=chatgpt.com)

# **ğŸ“ Section 1: Government & Public Procurement Portals**

# **Federal Procurement**

---

## **1\. System for Award Management (SAM.gov)**

**Overview:**  
SAM.gov is the primary database for vendors seeking to do business with the U.S. government. It consolidates several procurement systems into one, streamlining the registration process. â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/System_for_Award_Management)

**Registration Steps:**

1. **Obtain a Unique Entity Identifier (UEI):**  
   As of 2021, entities no longer require a DUNS number. Instead, SAM.gov issues a UEI upon registration.  
     
2. **Gather Necessary Information:**  
     
   * Legal business name and physical addressâ€‹  
   * Taxpayer Identification Number (TIN) or Employer Identification Number (EIN)â€‹  
   * Banking information for Electronic Funds Transfer (EFT)â€‹

   

3. **Complete the Registration:**  
   Visit [SAM.gov](https://sam.gov) and follow the prompts to register your entity. Ensure accuracy to prevent delays.  
     
4. **Update Annually:**  
   Renew your registration every 12 months to maintain active status.  
     
   ---

   ## **2\. GSA Schedule Contracts**

   **Overview:**  
   The General Services Administration (GSA) offers the GSA Schedule (also known as Federal Supply Schedule), a long-term government-wide contract with commercial firms to provide access to millions of commercial products and services at volume discount pricing. â€‹[en.wikipedia.org+1en.wikipedia.org+1](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_Services_Administration)  
     
   **Benefits:**  
     
* Streamlined procurement processâ€‹[en.wikipedia.org+1en.wikipedia.org+1](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GSA_Advantage)  
    
* Access to a vast network of federal customersâ€‹  
    
* Potential for increased salesâ€‹  
    
  **Steps to Obtain a GSA Schedule Contract:**  
    
1. **Determine Eligibility:**  
   Ensure your products or services align with GSA offerings.  
     
2. **Prepare Necessary Documentation:**  
     
   * Financial statementsâ€‹[axios.com+3en.wikipedia.org+3en.wikipedia.org+3](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GSA_Advantage)  
   * Past performance evaluationsâ€‹  
   * Pricing structuresâ€‹

   

3. **Submit an Offer:**  
   Utilize the GSA eOffer system to submit your proposal.  
     
4. **Negotiate Terms:**  
   Be prepared to discuss pricing and contract terms with a GSA contracting officer.  
     
5. **Award and Maintenance:**  
   Upon award, maintain compliance and update offerings as necessary.  
     
   ---

   ## **3\. Federal Procurement Data System (FPDS)**

   **Overview:**  
   FPDS is the central repository of information on federal contracting, providing data on contract actions over $3,000. â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Federal_Procurement_Data_System)  
     
   **Benefits:**  
     
* Market researchâ€‹  
    
* Competitive analysisâ€‹  
    
* Identifying procurement trendsâ€‹  
    
  **Accessing FPDS:**  
    
* Visit [FPDS.gov](https://www.fpds.gov/)â€‹  
    
* Utilize the search functions to explore contract data relevant to your industryâ€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **4\. NASA's Solutions for Enterprise-Wide Procurement (SEWP)**

  **Overview:**  
  NASA SEWP is a government-wide acquisition contract (GWAC) offering a wide range of information technology products and services. â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NASA_SEWP)  
    
  **Benefits:**  
    
* Access to IT and AV solutionsâ€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NASA_SEWP)  
    
* Streamlined acquisition processâ€‹  
    
* Opportunities across various federal agenciesâ€‹  
    
  **Becoming a SEWP Contract Holder:**  
    
1. **Monitor Opportunities:**  
   Keep an eye on [SEWP's official website](https://www.sewp.nasa.gov/) for upcoming contract opportunities.  
     
2. **Prepare Proposal:**  
   Align your offerings with SEWP requirements and submit a proposal during open solicitation periods.  
     
3. **Engage in Reverse Auctions:**  
   Participate in platforms like [Unison Marketplace](https://www.unisonglobal.com/), formerly FedBid, which facilitates reverse auctions for government contracts.  
     
   ---

   ## **5\. GSA Advantage\!**

   **Overview:**  
   GSA Advantage\! is an online shopping and ordering service created within the GSA for use by government agencies to buy commercial products and services. â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GSA_Advantage)  
     
   **Benefits:**  
     
* Visibility to federal purchasersâ€‹  
    
* Simplified purchasing processâ€‹  
    
* Access to a broad customer baseâ€‹  
    
  **Listing Products/Services:**  
    
1. **Obtain a GSA Schedule Contract:**  
   This is a prerequisite to listing on GSA Advantage\!.  
     
2. **Upload Offerings:**  
   Use the [GSA Advantage\! portal](https://www.gsaadvantage.gov/) to list your products or services.  
     
3. **Maintain Listings:**  
   Regularly update product information and pricing to remain competitive.  
     
   ---

   ## **1\. Federal Acquisition Regulation (FAR)**

   **Overview:**  
   The FAR is the principal set of rules governing all federal procurement processes in the United States. It standardizes contracting procedures across federal agencies, ensuring consistency and fairness.â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Federal_Acquisition_Regulation)  
     
   **Key Aspects:**  
     
* **Structure:**  
  The FAR is divided into 53 parts, each addressing different facets of the acquisition process, from definitions and administrative matters to specific contract requirements.â€‹  
    
* **Mandatory Clauses:**  
  Contracts often incorporate standard clauses from FAR Part 52\. Even if omitted, certain clauses may be considered included by law, a principle known as the "Christian Doctrine."â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Federal_Acquisition_Regulation)  
    
* **Compliance:**  
  Understanding and adhering to FAR provisions is crucial. Non-compliance can lead to contract disputes or terminations.â€‹  
    
  *Recommendation:*  
  Familiarize your team with the FAR, especially parts relevant to your services. Consider consulting with legal experts specializing in federal contracts to ensure compliance.â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **2\. General Services Administration (GSA) and the GSA Schedule**

  **Overview:**  
  The GSA manages federal property and provides contracting options for government agencies. One significant program is the GSA Schedule (also known as the Federal Supply Schedule), which offers pre-negotiated contracts for products and services.â€‹  
    
  **Benefits of GSA Schedule:**  
    
* **Streamlined Procurement:**  
  Agencies can purchase directly from pre-approved vendors, reducing procurement time.â€‹  
    
* **Increased Visibility:**  
  Being on the GSA Schedule can enhance your company's visibility to federal buyers.â€‹  
    
  **Steps to Obtain a GSA Schedule Contract:**  
    
1. **Determine Eligibility:**  
   Ensure your services align with those covered by the GSA Schedule.  
     
2. **Prepare Documentation:**  
   Gather financial records, past performance evaluations, and pricing structures.  
     
3. **Submit Proposal:**  
   Use the GSA eOffer system to submit your proposal.  
     
4. **Negotiation and Award:**  
   Engage in negotiations as needed before receiving the contract award.  
     
   *Recommendation:*  
   Given the complexity, consider attending GSA's training sessions or hiring a consultant experienced in GSA Schedule acquisitions.â€‹  
     
   ---

   ## **3\. Federal Procurement Data System (FPDS)**

   **Overview:**  
   The FPDS is the central repository of information on federal procurement actions. It provides transparency and allows vendors to analyze procurement trends.â€‹  
     
   **Uses:**  
     
* **Market Research:**  
  Identify which agencies procure services similar to yours and understand spending patterns.â€‹  
    
* **Competitive Analysis:**  
  Analyze competitors' federal contracts to strategize your bids.â€‹  
    
  *Recommendation:*  
  Regularly consult the FPDS to stay informed about procurement trends and identify potential opportunities.â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **4\. Simplified Acquisition Procedures (SAP)**

  **Overview:**  
  SAP streamlines the procurement process for acquisitions below a certain threshold, currently set at $250,000.â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simplified_Acquisition_Procedures)  
    
  **Advantages:**  
    
* **Simplified Process:**  
  Reduced administrative requirements make it easier for small businesses to participate.â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simplified_Acquisition_Procedures)  
    
* **Set-Asides:**  
  Many SAP procurements are reserved for small businesses, increasing your chances of winning a contract.â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simplified_Acquisition_Procedures)  
    
  *Recommendation:*  
  Monitor SAP opportunities on [SAM.gov](https://sam.gov) and be prepared to respond quickly due to shorter solicitation periods.â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **5\. Unison Marketplace (formerly FedBid)**

  **Overview:**  
  Unison Marketplace operates a reverse auction platform where government buyers post requirements, and vendors bid to fulfill them.â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FedBid)  
    
  **Benefits:**  
    
* **Competitive Bidding:**  
  Vendors can adjust bids in real-time to remain competitive.â€‹  
    
* **Transparency:**  
  The platform provides clear visibility into the bidding process.â€‹  
    
  *Recommendation:*  
  Register on Unison Marketplace to access and participate in reverse auctions relevant to your services.â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **6\. Recent Developments in Federal Procurement**

  **Policy Changes:**  
  The current administration has directed federal agencies to cease considering Diversity, Equity, and Inclusion (DEI) practices in procurement decisions. This reverses previous policies that factored DEI initiatives into contracting. â€‹[wsj.com](https://www.wsj.com/politics/policy/white-house-changes-federal-contracting-rules-to-eliminate-dei-considerations-141b9a44)  
    
  **Implications:**  
    
* **Contract Reviews:**  
  Existing contracts with DEI clauses may be renegotiated.â€‹[wsj.com](https://www.wsj.com/politics/policy/white-house-changes-federal-contracting-rules-to-eliminate-dei-considerations-141b9a44)  
    
* **Future Bids:**  
  Focus on core competencies and value propositions rather than DEI factors.â€‹  
    
  *Recommendation:*  
  Stay updated on policy changes to ensure compliance and adjust your bidding strategies accordingly.â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **7\. Additional Resources**

* **Federal Business Opportunities (FBO):**  
  While [FedBizOpps.gov](https://www.fbo.gov/) has been integrated into SAM.gov, it's essential to familiarize yourself with its functionalities for accessing federal procurement opportunities.â€‹  
    
* **Small Business Administration (SBA):**  
  The SBA offers resources and certifications that can enhance your competitiveness in federal contracting.â€‹  
    
  *Recommendation:*  
  Engage with local Procurement Technical Assistance Centers (PTACs) for personalized guidance on federal procurement processes.â€‹

  ## **1\. Unison Marketplace (Formerly FedBid)**

  **Overview:**  
  Unison Marketplace operates a full-service online reverse auction platform where government agencies post procurement requirements, and vendors competitively bid to fulfill them. This platform is utilized by numerous federal, state, and local government entities to procure a wide range of goods and services. â€‹  
    
  **Benefits:**  
    
* **Competitive Bidding:**  
  Vendors can submit bids in a dynamic environment, potentially securing contracts at favorable terms.â€‹  
    
* **Transparency:**  
  The reverse auction format provides clear visibility into the bidding process, fostering fair competition.â€‹  
    
  **Action Steps:**  
    
* **Register as a Vendor:**  
  Visit the [Unison Marketplace website](https://www.unisonmarketplace.com/) to create a vendor account.â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FedBid)  
    
* **Participate in Auctions:**  
  Regularly monitor and bid on relevant procurement opportunities to expand your federal contracting portfolio.â€‹

  ## **5\. Naval Facilities Engineering Systems Command (NAVFAC)**

  **Overview:**  
  NAVFAC manages the planning, design, and construction of shore facilities for the U.S. Navy and Marine Corps, presenting various contracting opportunities.â€‹  
    
  **Action Steps:**  
    
* **Explore Contracting Opportunities:**  
  Visit the [NAVFAC Contracting page](https://www.navfac.navy.mil/Business-Lines/Contracting/) to view current solicitations and procurement forecasts.â€‹[usace.army.mil](https://www.usace.army.mil/Business-With-Us/)  
    
* **Attend Industry Forums:**  
  Participate in NAVFAC-hosted industry forums and outreach events to network and gain insights into upcoming projects.â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **6\. Defense Logistics Agency Internet Bid Board System (DIBBS)**

  **Overview:**  
  DIBBS is an online portal where the Defense Logistics Agency (DLA) posts solicitations for various supplies and services, including those related to defense projects.â€‹  
    
  **Action Steps:**  
    
* **Register on DIBBS:**  
  Create an account on the [DIBBS website](https://www.dibbs.bsm.dla.mil/) to access solicitations and submit bids.â€‹  
    
* **Monitor Solicitations:**  
  Regularly check DIBBS for new opportunities that align with Scan2Plan's capabilities.â€‹

  # **State & Local Procurement**

  ### 

  ### **Guiding Principles**

  **Objective:** Establish a **universal framework** for Scan2Plan to register and prequalify with **state and local government procurement portals** before diving into **state-specific** registrations.  
    
  ---

  ## **1\. Understanding State & Local Procurement Structures**

  ### **A. Types of State & Local Procurement Entities**

1. **State-Level Procurement Agencies** â€“ Manage **statewide contracts** for government buildings, transportation, and public works.  
     
   * Example: **California Department of General Services (DGS), Texas Comptroller's State Procurement Division.**

   

2. **Local Government Agencies** â€“ Handle **city, county, and municipal contracts** for public infrastructure, facilities, and maintenance.  
     
   * Example: **City of New York Procurement, Los Angeles County Vendor Registration.**

   

3. **Public Works & Infrastructure Agencies** â€“ Oversee **construction, maintenance, and expansion** of public facilities.  
     
   * Example: **Illinois Department of Transportation, Washington State Public Works Board.**

   

4. **Educational Institutions** â€“ Includes **public school districts, universities, and community colleges.**

   * ## Example: **State University Procurement Systems (e.g., SUNY, UC, Texas A\&M), K-12 district purchasing co-ops.**

     ## **2\. Key Registration & Prequalification Portals**

     ### **A. Statewide Procurement Portals (Most States Have One)**

     Each state has a **central procurement portal** where vendors **must register** to bid on projects. These portals are often called:

   

* **"eProcurement" Systems**  
    
* **"Supplier Registration Portals"**  
    
* **"Vendor Self-Service" Systems (VSS)**  
    
  **Examples:**  
    
* **California eProcure (CaleProcure) â†’ [https://caleprocure.ca.gov/](https://caleprocure.ca.gov/)**  
    
* **Texas SmartBuy â†’ [https://comptroller.texas.gov/purchasing/](https://comptroller.texas.gov/purchasing/)**  
    
* **Florida MyFloridaMarketPlace (MFMP) â†’ [https://vendor.myfloridamarketplace.com/](https://vendor.myfloridamarketplace.com/)**  
    
* **New York State Contract System (NYSCS) â†’ [https://ny.newnycontracts.com/](https://ny.newnycontracts.com/)**

  ### **B. Cooperative Purchasing Organizations (Multi-State Access)**

  These organizations allow vendors to **register once** and access **multiple state & local contracts** in different jurisdictions.  
    
1. **NASPO ValuePoint (National Association of State Procurement Officials)**  
     
   * Covers **48 states** \+ local governments.  
   * Register at: [**https://www.naspovaluepoint.org/**](https://www.naspovaluepoint.org/)

   

2. **Sourcewell**  
     
   * Cooperative procurement for **government, education, and non-profits** across the U.S.  
   * Register at: [**https://www.sourcewell-mn.gov/**](https://www.sourcewell-mn.gov/)

   

3. **Omnia Partners (Public & Private Sector)**  
     
   * One of the largest **cooperative purchasing groups**.  
   * Register at: [**https://www.omniapartners.com/**](https://www.omniapartners.com/)

   

4. **E\&I Cooperative Services** (Education & Higher Ed)  
     
   * Focused on **universities, school districts, and research facilities.**  
   * Register at: [**https://www.eandi.org/**](https://www.eandi.org/)

   

5. **HGACBuy (Houston-Galveston Area Council)**  
     
   * Regional cooperative serving **local governments across multiple states**.

   * ## Register at: [**https://www.hgacbuy.org/**](https://www.hgacbuy.org/)

     ## **3\. General Prequalification Steps for Any State/Local Agency**

     ### **A. Obtain Required Business Registrations & Certifications**

     Before registering as a vendor, **some states require additional credentials:**

   

6. **Business Entity Registration** â€“ Register with the **Secretary of State** where you want to do business.  
     
   * Example: **Texas Secretary of State Business Registration.**

   

7. **Sales Tax ID (If Applicable)** â€“ Some states require a **State Tax ID** for contracts involving taxable sales.  
     
8. **Small & Minority Business Certifications (If Applicable)**  
     
   * **Disadvantaged Business Enterprise (DBE) Certification** â€“ For **state-funded transportation projects.**  
       
   * **Minority/Women Business Enterprise (MWBE) Certification** â€“ Some states have MWBE participation requirements.  
       
   * **Small Business Enterprise (SBE) Certification** â€“ Some states have **small business set-asides**.

     ### **B. Register on the State's eProcurement System**

* Each state has a **vendor registration process** through its **procurement portal**.  
    
* Most require:  
    
  * **Business Information** (EIN, Legal Name, Address).  
      
  * **Financial & Tax Information** (Bank Account, W9).  
      
  * **Certifications (If Applicable).**

    ### **C. Review & Respond to Bid Opportunities**

* Once registered, vendors can **search RFPs/RFQs** on **state/local portals**.  
    
* Some states require **prequalification** for large construction or service contracts.  
    
  ---

  ## **4\. Strategies to Prioritize State & Local Registration**

  ### **A. Start with High-Procurement States**

* **Top states by government spending:**  
    
  1. **California** â€“ Largest procurement market ($10B+ annually).  
       
  2. **Texas** â€“ Strong infrastructure & municipal projects.  
       
  3. **New York** â€“ High volume of public works projects.  
       
  4. **Florida** â€“ Major education & transportation spending.  
       
  5. **Illinois** â€“ Heavy investment in government facilities.

     ### **B. Focus on Local & County Governments in Targeted Metro Areas**

* Many **major city/county agencies** manage their own procurement:  
    
  * **Los Angeles County Vendor Portal**  
      
  * **Chicago Procurement Services**  
      
  * **Miami-Dade Vendor Registration**  
      
  * **Houston Procurement Division**

    ### **C. Leverage Cooperative Purchasing to Expand Access**

* **Start with NASPO, Sourcewell, and Omnia Partners** â†’ These provide access to **multi-state** opportunities.  
    
  ---

  ## **1\. NASPO ValuePoint**

  **Overview:**  
  NASPO ValuePoint is the cooperative purchasing arm of the National Association of State Procurement Officials (NASPO), offering competitively sourced contracts to state and local governments.â€‹[xerox.com+3naspovaluepoint.org+3naspo.org+3](https://www.naspovaluepoint.org/cooperative-contracts/)  
    
  **Process to Become a Supplier:**  
    
* **Monitor Solicitations:**  
  NASPO ValuePoint does not have a standard vendor registration process. Instead, they release Requests for Proposals (RFPs) through lead states. To participate:â€‹[doa.wi.gov+4naspovaluepoint.org+4naspo.org+4](https://www.naspovaluepoint.org/future-suppliers/)  
    
  * **Check Current Solicitations:**  
    Regularly visit the Current Solicitations page to view active opportunities.  
      
  * **Respond to Relevant RFPs:**  
    Submit proposals for solicitations that align with Scan2Plan's services.


* **Partner with Existing Contractors:**  
  If a relevant contract is already awarded, consider partnering with current NASPO ValuePoint contractors as authorized distributors or service providers. â€‹[naspovaluepoint.org+2naspo.org+2naspovaluepoint.org+2](https://www.naspo.org/suppliers/faqs/)  
    
  **Additional Resources:**  
    
* **Future Suppliers Information:**  
  Visit the [Future Suppliers page](https://www.naspovaluepoint.org/future-suppliers/) for insights into becoming a NASPO ValuePoint contractor.â€‹[naspovaluepoint.org+1naspo.org+1](https://www.naspovaluepoint.org/future-suppliers/)  
    
* **Supplier FAQs:**  
  Review the [Supplier FAQs](https://www.naspo.org/suppliers/faqs/) for common questions and detailed guidance.â€‹[naspo.org+2naspo.org+2naspo.org+2](https://www.naspo.org/suppliers/faqs/)  
    
  ---

  ## **2\. Sourcewell**

  **Overview:**  
  Sourcewell is a government agency offering cooperative purchasing solutions for education, government, and nonprofit entities.â€‹[apsu.edu+1xerox.com+1](https://www.apsu.edu/procurement/employees/cooperatives.php)  
    
  **Process to Become a Supplier:**  
    
* **Respond to Open Solicitations:**  
  Sourcewell utilizes a competitive solicitation process to establish contracts:â€‹  
    
  * **View Open RFPs:**  
    Access current opportunities on the Sourcewell Procurement Portal.  
      
  * **Submit Proposals:**  
    Follow the instructions provided in each RFP to submit a compliant proposal.


* **Await Award Notification:**  
  After evaluation, Sourcewell will notify successful vendors and establish contracts.â€‹  
    
  **Additional Resources:**  
    
* **Become a Supplier:**  
  Detailed information is available on the [Become a Supplier page](https://www.sourcewell-mn.gov/sourcewell-for-vendors/become-a-supplier).â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **3\. OMNIA Partners**

  **Overview:**  
  OMNIA Partners is a leading cooperative purchasing organization for public and private sector procurement.â€‹[procurement.ucf.edu](https://procurement.ucf.edu/links-useful-links/)  
    
  **Process to Become a Supplier:**  
    
* **Participate in Solicitations:**  
  OMNIA Partners establishes contracts through competitive solicitations:â€‹  
    
  * **Check Solicitation Opportunities:**  
    Visit the Suppliers page to learn about upcoming solicitations.  
      
  * **Submit Responses:**  
    Provide detailed proposals in response to solicitations that match Scan2Plan's offerings.


* **Engage in Contract Negotiations:**  
  If selected, engage in negotiations to finalize contract terms.â€‹  
    
  **Additional Resources:**  
    
* **Supplier Overview:**  
  More information is available on the [Become a Supplier page](https://www.omniapartners.com/suppliers/become-a-supplier).â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **4\. E\&I Cooperative Services**

  **Overview:**  
  E\&I Cooperative Services is a member-owned, nonprofit sourcing cooperative focused on the educational sector.â€‹[xerox.com](https://www.xerox.com/en-us/services/government-solutions/cooperative-purchasing)  
    
  **Process to Become a Supplier:**  
    
* **Respond to RFPs:**  
  E\&I conducts competitive solicitations to establish contracts:â€‹  
    
  * **Access Open Solicitations:**  
    Visit the Supplier Opportunities page to view active RFPs.  
      
  * **Submit Proposals:**  
    Follow the guidelines outlined in each RFP to participate in the bidding process.


* **Contract Award:**  
  Successful bidders will enter into contracts to serve E\&I's member institutions.â€‹[xerox.com](https://www.xerox.com/en-us/services/government-solutions/cooperative-purchasing)  
    
  **Additional Resources:**  
    
* **Become a Supplier:**  
  Detailed guidance is available on the [Become a Supplier page](https://www.eandi.org/suppliers/become-a-supplier/).â€‹  
    
  ---

    
  **Recommendations for Scan2Plan:**  
    
* **Regularly Monitor Solicitations:**  
  Each cooperative releases RFPs based on their members' needs. Regularly checking their procurement portals ensures timely responses.â€‹  
    
* **Prepare Comprehensive Proposals:**  
  Ensure that all submissions are thorough, address all requirements, and highlight Scan2Plan's unique value propositions.â€‹  
    
* **Consider Strategic Partnerships:**  
  If direct contracts are not immediately attainable, partnering with existing contractors can provide an entry point into these cooperatives.â€‹  
    
  By engaging with these cooperatives, Scan2Plan can significantly expand its reach within the public procurement landscape, accessing a broad network of potential clients across various sectors.

  # **State-by-State Procurement Portals**

  # **Alabama**

* **Alabama Department of Finance â€“ Division of Purchasing**: [https://purchasing.alabama.gov/â€‹](https://purchasing.alabama.gov/â€‹)  
    
  â€‹To engage in procurement opportunities with the State of Alabama, vendors must navigate the state's procurement systems effectively. Here's a detailed guide to assist you:â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **1\. Alabama Buys: The E-Procurement System**

  **Overview:**  
    
  Alabama Buys is the state's official e-procurement platform, facilitating interactions between vendors and state agencies. It streamlines processes such as bid notifications, submissions, and contract management.â€‹[reab.alabama.gov+1procurement.staars.alabama.gov+1](https://reab.alabama.gov/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/RFP.pdf)  
    
  **Access:**  
    
* **Website:** [Alabama Buys](https://alabamabuys.gov/)â€‹[procurement.staars.alabama.gov+2reab.alabama.gov+2procurement.staars.alabama.gov+2](https://reab.alabama.gov/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/RFP.pdf)  
    
  **Features:**  
    
* **Vendor Registration:** Allows vendors to create and manage their profiles.â€‹[vendors.alabama.gov+2procurement.staars.alabama.gov+2vendors.alabama.gov+2](https://procurement.staars.alabama.gov/PRDVSS1X1/AltSelfService)  
    
* **Bid Opportunities:** Provides access to current solicitations and the ability to submit responses electronically.â€‹  
    
* **Contract Management:** Enables vendors to view and manage awarded contracts.â€‹[vendors.alabama.gov](https://vendors.alabama.gov/docs/VSSGuide.pdf)  
    
  ---

  ## **2\. STAARS Vendor Self Service (VSS): Legacy System**

  **Overview:**  
    
  Prior to Alabama Buys, the State utilized the STAARS VSS platform for procurement activities. While Alabama Buys is now the primary system, some functions or historical data may still be accessed through STAARS VSS.â€‹[vendors.alabama.gov+5procurement.staars.alabama.gov+5vendors.alabama.gov+5](https://procurement.staars.alabama.gov/PRDVSS1X1/AltSelfService)  
    
  **Access:**  
    
* **Website:** [STAARS VSS](https://procurement.staars.alabama.gov/PRDVSS1X1/AltSelfService)â€‹[procurement.staars.alabama.gov+4procurement.staars.alabama.gov+4medicaid.alabama.gov+4](https://procurement.staars.alabama.gov/PRDVSS1X1/AltSelfService)  
    
  **Important Note:**  
    
  As of June 28, 2021, Alabama's E-Procurement System, Alabama Buys, is live and can be accessed at [Alabama Buys](https://alabamabuys.gov/). All vendors doing business through the Department of Finance Division of Purchasing should access Alabama Buys. Agencies are being migrated to Alabama Buys in phases, with all agencies expected to transition by October 1, 2021\. â€‹[reab.alabama.gov+2procurement.staars.alabama.gov+2procurement.staars.alabama.gov+2](https://procurement.staars.alabama.gov/PRDVSS1X1/AltSelfService)[procurement.staars.alabama.gov+1procurement.staars.alabama.gov+1](https://procurement.staars.alabama.gov/LoginExternal/Pages/LoginAnnouncements.html)  
    
  ---

  ## **3\. Vendor Registration Process**

  **Steps to Register:**  
    
1. **Access Alabama Buys:**  
     
   * Navigate to the [Alabama Buys](https://alabamabuys.gov/) portal.â€‹

   

2. **Initiate Registration:**  
     
   * Click on "New Supplier Registration" and complete all mandatory fields marked with an asterisk (\*).â€‹[reab.alabama.gov](https://reab.alabama.gov/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/RFP.pdf)

   

3. **Commodity Codes:**  
     
   * During registration, specify the commodities your business offers using the National Institute of Governmental Purchasing (NIGP) Commodity Codes. This ensures you receive relevant bid notifications. â€‹[vendors.alabama.gov+2naspo.org+2vendors.alabama.gov+2](https://www.naspo.org/states/alabama/)

   

4. **Submission and Approval:**  
     
   * After completing the registration, submit it for approval. You will receive an email notification regarding the status of your registration.â€‹  
     **Registration Fee:**

   

* Vendors are required to pay a bi-annual registration fee of $200. This fee must be paid electronically during the registration process. â€‹[casetext.com](https://casetext.com/regulation/alabama-administrative-code/title-355-state-of-alabama-department-of-finance/chapter-355-4-1-division-of-purchasing/section-355-4-1-03-general-requirements-of-vendors)  
    
  ---

  ## **4\. Bid Opportunities and Notifications**

  **Accessing Bid Opportunities:**  
    
* Once registered, vendors can access and respond to Invitations to Bid (ITBs) and Requests for Proposals (RFPs) through the Alabama Buys portal.â€‹  
    
  **Notifications:**  
    
* Registered vendors receive email notifications about relevant bid opportunities based on their selected commodity codes.â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **5\. Additional Resources**

* **Vendor Information:**  
    
  * For comprehensive guidelines, refer to the [Vendor Information](https://comptroller.alabama.gov/vendor-information/) page.â€‹[comptroller.alabama.gov+1vendors.alabama.gov+1](https://comptroller.alabama.gov/vendor-information/)


* **Vendor Self Service Guide:**

  * ## Detailed instructions on using the VSS system are available in the [Vendor Self Service Guide](https://vendors.alabama.gov/docs/VSSGuide.pdf).â€‹[procurement.staars.alabama.gov+3vendors.alabama.gov+3vendors.alabama.gov+3](https://vendors.alabama.gov/docs/VSSGuide.pdf)

    By following these steps and utilizing the provided resources, vendors can effectively engage with Alabama's procurement processes and explore business opportunities with state agencies.â€‹[procurement.staars.alabama.gov](https://procurement.staars.alabama.gov/PRDVSS1X1/AltSelfService)

    # **Alaska**

* **Alaska Department of Administration â€“ Division of General Services**: [http://doa.alaska.gov/dgs/â€‹](http://doa.alaska.gov/dgs/â€‹)  
    
  â€‹Engaging with the State of Alaska's procurement processes involves understanding and navigating several key platforms and procedures. Here's a comprehensive guide to assist you:â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **1\. Office of Procurement and Property Management (OPPM)**

  **Overview:**  
    
  The OPPM serves as Alaska's centralized authority for procurement and property management, ensuring compliance with the State Procurement Code. It offers support to state entities, municipalities, and public corporations in acquiring goods and services efficiently. â€‹[oppm.doa.alaska.gov](https://oppm.doa.alaska.gov/home/)  
    
  **Key Functions:**  
    
* **Statewide Contracting:** Assists in establishing cost-effective contracts and agreements.â€‹  
    
* **Procurement Officer Certification:** Manages training programs to uphold professionalism in state procurement operations.â€‹[aws.state.ak.us+1oppm.doa.alaska.gov+1](https://aws.state.ak.us/TrainAlaska/)  
    
* **Property Management:** Oversees the lifecycle of state property, including surplus programs.â€‹  
    
  **Resources:**  
    
* **Vendor Resources:** Provides guidance on doing business with the state, accessible at the [Vendor Resources page](https://oppm.doa.alaska.gov/vendor-resources/).â€‹[oppm.doa.alaska.gov](https://oppm.doa.alaska.gov/vendor-resources/)  
    
* **Purchasing Documents:** Offers necessary forms and references for procurement activities, available on the [Purchasing Documents and Forms page](https://oppm.doa.alaska.gov/purchasing/documents-and-forms/).â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **2\. Vendor Self Service (VSS) Portal**

  **Overview:**  
    
  The VSS portal is Alaska's platform for vendors to manage their profiles, access solicitation information, and track payments. It integrates with the state's financial and procurement system, IRIS (Integrated Resource Information System). â€‹[static1.squarespace.com+2doa.alaska.gov+2aws.state.ak.us+2](https://doa.alaska.gov/dof/iris/)  
    
  **Registration Process:**  
    
1. **Access the VSS Portal:**  
     
   * Navigate to the [VSS Portal](https://iris-vss.alaska.gov/).â€‹[youtube.com](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9rXBYKX41Bs)

   

2. **Create a New Account:**  
     
   * Select "Register" and follow the prompts to provide business information.â€‹

   

3. **Commodity Codes:**  
     
   * During registration, specify the commodities your business offers using the National Institute of Governmental Purchasing (NIGP) Commodity Codes.â€‹

   

4. **Submission and Approval:**  
     
   * After completing the registration, submit it for approval. You will receive an email notification regarding the status of your registration.â€‹  
     **Assistance:**

   

* **Vendor Registration Instructions:** Detailed guidance is available in the [Vendor Registration Instructions document](https://dot.alaska.gov/procurement/BSOinstructions.pdf).â€‹[dot.alaska.gov+1dot.alaska.gov+1](https://dot.alaska.gov/procurement/BSOinstructions.pdf)  
    
* **Video Tutorial:** A step-by-step video is accessible on [YouTube](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9rXBYKX41Bs).â€‹[youtube.com](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9rXBYKX41Bs)  
    
  ---

  ## **3\. Online Public Notices**

  **Overview:**  
    
  Alaska's Online Public Notices system publishes current solicitations, bid opportunities, and procurement announcements. â€‹[dot.alaska.gov+4aws.state.ak.us+4aws.state.ak.us+4](https://aws.state.ak.us/OnlinePublicNotices/)  
    
  **Access:**  
    
* **Website:** Visit the [Online Public Notices page](https://aws.state.ak.us/OnlinePublicNotices/).â€‹[aws.state.ak.us+3aws.state.ak.us+3aws.state.ak.us+3](https://aws.state.ak.us/OnlinePublicNotices/)  
    
  **Features:**  
    
* **Search Functionality:** Allows vendors to filter notices by category, department, or date.â€‹  
    
* **Subscription Service:** Vendors can subscribe to receive notifications about new opportunities.â€‹  
    
  ---

  ## **4\. Department of Transportation & Public Facilities (DOT\&PF) Procurement**

  **Overview:**  
    
  The DOT\&PF manages procurement for transportation and public facility projects, including construction and maintenance contracts. â€‹[dot.alaska.gov+2dot.alaska.gov+2dot.alaska.gov+2](https://dot.alaska.gov/procurement/index.shtml)  
    
  **Key Areas:**  
    
* **Supply and Services:** Handles procurement of goods and non-professional services.â€‹  
    
* **Construction Bidding:** Manages the bidding process for construction projects.â€‹  
    
  **Resources:**  
    
* **Bidder Registration:** Vendors must submit the [Bidder Registration Form](https://dot.alaska.gov/cvlrts/bidreg/bidreg.html) annually to participate in bidding.â€‹[dot.alaska.gov](https://dot.alaska.gov/cvlrts/bidreg/bidreg.html)  
    
* **Contractor Information:** Detailed bidding information is available on the [Contractor Bidding Information page](https://dot.alaska.gov/procurement/bidding/biddinginfo/index.shtml).â€‹[dot.alaska.gov](https://dot.alaska.gov/procurement/bidding/biddinginfo/index.shtml)  
    
  ---

    
  **Recommendations for Scan2Plan:**  
    
* **Complete Vendor Registration:** Ensure that Scan2Plan is registered in the VSS portal to access and respond to solicitations.â€‹  
    
* **Monitor Public Notices:** Regularly check the Online Public Notices for relevant procurement opportunities.â€‹[dot.alaska.gov+4aws.state.ak.us+4aws.state.ak.us+4](https://aws.state.ak.us/OnlinePublicNotices/)  
    
* **Engage with DOT\&PF:** Given the nature of Scan2Plan's services, collaborating with the DOT\&PF may present significant opportunities in infrastructure projects.

  # **Arizona**

  ## **2\. State Procurement Office (SPO)**

  **Key Functions:**

  ## **3\. Registration Process**

  **Steps to Register:**

   * During registration, specify the commodities your business offers to receive relevant bid notifications.â€‹

  # **Florida**

  ## **1\. State-Level Procurement: MyFloridaMarketPlace (MFMP)**

  **Overview:**  
    
  MyFloridaMarketPlace (MFMP) is Florida's official eProcurement system, connecting vendors with state government organizations for purchasing goods and services. The MFMP Vendor Information Portal (VIP) allows vendors to register, receive electronic purchase orders, and access information on upcoming bids. â€‹[vendor.myfloridamarketplace.com](https://vendor.myfloridamarketplace.com/)  
    
  **Access:**  
    
* **Website:** [MFMP Vendor Information Portal](https://vendor.myfloridamarketplace.com/)â€‹  
    
  **Registration Process:**  
    
1. **Create a New MFMP VIP Account:**  
     
   * Visit the [MFMP VIP registration page](https://vendor.myfloridamarketplace.com/register).â€‹  
       
   * Complete the "New Vendor Registration" section by entering your company name, tax ID type (FEIN, Foreign, or SSN), and tax ID.â€‹

   

2. **Complete Registration Details:**  
     
   * Provide general business information, address, and contact details as prompted.â€‹  
       
   * Ensure you have your tax filing information, including the business name as it appears on your 1099 tax form.â€‹

   

3. **Submit a Substitute W-9:**  
     
   * The Florida Department of Financial Services (DFS) requires vendors to have a valid Form W-9 on file before releasing payments.â€‹  
       
   * Submit your W-9 electronically through the [State of Florida Vendor Portal](https://flvendor.myfloridacfo.com/).â€‹[fdot.gov](https://www.fdot.gov/procurement/VendorOneStopQuickLinks.shtm)

   

4. **Finalize Registration:**  
     
   * Review all entered information and submit your registration.â€‹  
       
   * You will receive a confirmation email upon successful registration.â€‹  
       
     **Assistance:**

     
* **MFMP Vendor Guide:** A comprehensive guide is available to assist with the registration process.â€‹  
    
* **Contact:** For support, call the MFMP helpdesk at 1-866-352-3776.â€‹

   * A valid credit card is required for the $12 annual fee.â€‹[vendors.ehawaii.gov](https://vendors.ehawaii.gov/hce/)

  ## **1\. State-Level Procurement: Idaho Division of Purchasing**

  **Overview:**  
    
  The Idaho Division of Purchasing (DOP) serves as the central procurement authority for the state, responsible for establishing procurement policies and procuring goods and services for most executive agencies.   **Access:**

  **Registration Process:**  
    
1. **IPRO Vendor Registration:**  
     
   * Vendors must register in the Idaho eProcurement System (IPRO) to access detailed solicitation information and be eligible for contract awards. â€‹[purchasing.idaho.gov+2purchasing.idaho.gov+2purchasing.idaho.gov+2](https://purchasing.idaho.gov/helpie_faq/ipro-registration-training-2/)  
       
   * **Steps to Register:**  
       
     * Visit the IPRO Supplier Portal.  
         
     * Click on "Register" and provide the required business information, including contact details and commodity codes relevant to your offerings.  
         
     * Registration is free and typically takes only a few moments.

     

   * **Assistance:**  
       
     * For questions or assistance with IPRO registration, contact the Division of Purchasing at (208) 327-7465 or email [purchasing@adm.idaho.gov](mailto:purchasing@adm.idaho.gov).

   

2. **Luma System:**

  ## **1\. State-Level Procurement: Indiana Department of Administration (IDOA) Supplier Portal**

   * Visit the [Bidder Profile Registration page](https://www.in.gov/idoa/procurement/supplier-resource-center/requirements-to-do-business-with-the-state/bidder-profile-registration/).â€‹[faqs.in.gov+9faqs.in.gov+9in.gov+9](https://faqs.in.gov/hc/en-us/articles/15550113052820-What-should-I-do-if-I-can-t-get-signed-into-the-Supplier-Portal)

     * View and respond to current bidding opportunities.  
         
     * Update your bidder profile.  
         
     * Report Prime Contractor or certified Subcontractor contractual payments.  
         
     * Complete and submit the Buy Indiana and Supplier Diversity Applications.  
         
     * Submit the Affirmation of Continued Eligibility (ACE) Form.

     

     **Assistance:**

* **Review/Evaluation Process:** Describes the methodologies for evaluating bids and proposals.â€‹

    ## **2\. Legal Framework: Chapter 30B \- The Uniform Procurement Act**

    **Overview:**  
    Chapter 30B, known as the Uniform Procurement Act, establishes uniform procedures for local government procurement of supplies, services, and real property. The law aims to promote competition, ensure fair and open processes, and enhance public confidence in government procurement. â€‹[malegislature.gov+2mass.gov+2mass.gov+2](https://www.mass.gov/info-details/about-chapter-30b-the-uniform-procurement-act)  
    **Key Provisions:**

    
* **Application:** Chapter 30B applies to the procurement of supplies and services by local governmental bodies, with specific procedures based on contract value.â€‹  
    
* **Procedures:** The Act outlines different procurement procedures, such as competitive sealed bidding and requests for proposals, depending on the nature and value of the contract.â€‹[malegislature.gov](https://malegislature.gov/Laws/GeneralLaws/PartI/TitleIII/Chapter30B)  
    
  **Access:**  
    
* **Full Text:** [Chapter 30B \- Massachusetts Legislature](https://malegislature.gov/Laws/GeneralLaws/PartI/TitleIII/Chapter30B)â€‹[malegislature.gov](https://malegislature.gov/Laws/GeneralLaws/PartI/TitleIII/Chapter30B)  
    
  **Resources:**  
    
* **Chapter 30B Manual:** This manual provides detailed guidance on procurement requirements and recommendations. â€‹[mass.gov](https://www.mass.gov/lists/oig-public-procurement-forms-guides-and-advisories)  
    
  ---

    ## **2\. Vendor Resources and Opportunities**

    ## **Contract Connect:**     DTMB's Contract Connect website provides information to vendors interested in doing business with the State of Michigan. It offers resources such as how to register as a vendor, bid proposals, commodity codes, and access to the Vendor Innovation Portal. â€‹[michigan.gov+8michigan.gov+8michigan.gov+8](https://www.michigan.gov/dtmb/procurement/contractconnect/lets-do-business)     **Vendor Opportunity Dashboard:**     The Vendor Opportunity Dashboard offers a visual representation of upcoming procurement opportunities, allowing vendors to search and filter projects by description, estimated post date, and sourcing category. This tool helps vendors identify potential opportunities and plan accordingly. â€‹[michigan.gov](https://www.michigan.gov/dtmb/procurement/contractconnect/vendor-opportunity-dashboard)     **MiDEAL Extended Purchasing Program:**     MiDEAL allows local units of government, such as schools, cities, counties, and nonprofits, to use state contracts to buy goods and services. Vendors with state contracts that include extended purchasing language can participate in the MiDEAL program, expanding their customer base. â€‹[michigan.gov+3en.wikipedia.org+3michigan.gov+3](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michigan_Department_of_Technology%2C_Management_and_Budget)[michigan.gov](https://www.michigan.gov/dtmb/procurement/mideal-extended-purchasing-program/vendor-center)     **Vendor Innovation Portal:**     The Vendor Innovation Portal enables businesses to share innovative and cost-saving products and services with the State of Michigan, especially those related to information technology. Submissions may lead to formal presentations to state leadership teams. â€‹[michigan.gov](https://www.michigan.gov/dtmb/procurement/contractconnect/vendor-innovation-portal)

  â€‹Engaging with Michigan's municipal procurement processes involves understanding the platforms used by various local governments to manage their purchasing activities. One prominent platform facilitating procurement across numerous Michigan municipalities is the **Michigan Inter-governmental Trade Network (MITN) Purchasing Group**.â€‹[bidnetdirect.com](https://www.bidnetdirect.com/MITN)  
    
  **Michigan Inter-governmental Trade Network (MITN) Purchasing Group:**  
    
* **Overview:** MITN is a collaborative procurement platform that connects nearly 200 local government purchasing departments within Michigan. It centralizes bid opportunities, requests for proposals (RFPs), and awarded contracts, providing vendors with a streamlined process to access and respond to municipal procurement opportunities.â€‹  
    
* **Access:**  
    
  1. **Website:** [MITN Purchasing Group](https://www.bidnetdirect.com/mitn)â€‹[bidnetdirect.com+1en.wikipedia.org+1](https://www.bidnetdirect.com/MITN)


* **Registration Process:**  
    
  1. **Vendor Registration:**  
       
     * Visit the MITN Vendor Registration page.  
     * Complete the registration by providing necessary business information, including contact details and relevant documentation.  
     * Once registered, vendors can access bid information and documents, receive notifications of matching bids, and submit responses electronically.

     

     **Benefits of Using MITN:**


* **Centralized Access:** Vendors gain access to a wide array of procurement opportunities from multiple Michigan local governments through a single platform.â€‹  
    
* **Notification Services:** Registered vendors receive alerts about new bids and RFPs that match their specified products or services, ensuring they don't miss relevant opportunities.â€‹  
    
* **Document Management:** The platform allows vendors to download necessary documents and submit their proposals electronically, simplifying the procurement process.â€‹  
    
  **Recommendations for Scan2Plan:**  
    
* **Register on MITN:** To access a broad spectrum of municipal procurement opportunities in Michigan, Scan2Plan should register as a vendor on the MITN Purchasing Group platform.â€‹[bidnetdirect.com](https://www.bidnetdirect.com/MITN)  
    
* **Set Up Notifications:** Configure the account to receive notifications for bids and RFPs relevant to Scan2Plan's services to stay informed about new opportunities.â€‹  
    
* **Monitor Opportunities:** Regularly log in to the MITN platform to review and respond to open solicitations that align with Scan2Plan's expertise.â€‹  
    
  By leveraging the MITN Purchasing Group, Scan2Plan can efficiently navigate Michigan's municipal procurement landscape and identify opportunities that align with its business objectives

  # **Missouri**

* **MissouriBUYS**: [https://missouribuys.mo.gov/â€‹](https://missouribuys.mo.gov/â€‹)

  ## **1\. State-Level Procurement: MissouriBUYS eProcurement System**

  **Overview:**  
    
  MissouriBUYS is the State of Missouri's secure, user-friendly, web-based statewide eProcurement system. It serves as a one-stop shop for procurements by state government agencies and includes supplier (vendor) self-service registration, solicitation postings, online bidding, and order management. As of May 2024, the state began its transition to "MissouriBUYS, powered by MOVERS," opening a new Self-Service Supplier Registration Portal. â€‹  
    
  **Access:**  
    
* **Website:** [MissouriBUYS Statewide eProcurement System](https://missouribuys.mo.gov/)â€‹  
    
  **Registration Process:**  
    
1. **Supplier Registration:**  
     
   * Visit the [Supplier Registration page](https://missouribuys.mo.gov/supplier-registration).â€‹  
       
   * Complete the registration form by providing necessary business information, including contact details and relevant documentation.â€‹  
       
   * Once registered, vendors can receive notifications of bid opportunities, submit proposals electronically, and manage their profiles.â€‹  
       
     **Bid Opportunities:**

     
* Current bid opportunities are posted on the MissouriBUYS Bid Board. With the state's transition to the new system, solicitations issued on or after September 18, 2024, can be found on the new MissouriBUYS, powered by MOVERS Bid Board. â€‹  
    
  **Assistance:**  
    
* **MissouriBUYS Help Desk:**  
    
  * **Phone:** (573) 751-2387â€‹  
      
  * **Email:** [purchmail@oa.mo.gov](mailto:purchmail@oa.mo.gov)â€‹[purch.oa.mo.gov+5purch.oa.mo.gov+5purch.oa.mo.gov+5](https://purch.oa.mo.gov/)  
      
    ---

    ## **2\. Cooperative Procurement Program**

    **Overview:**  
    Missouri State Statutes (Chapters 34, 37, and 67\) authorize the Division of Purchasing to conduct a cooperative purchasing program. This program allows eligible local governments, political subdivisions, and quasi-public governmental bodies to participate in the state's procurement contracts, thereby leveraging collective buying power for cost savings. â€‹[missouribuys.mo.gov](https://missouribuys.mo.gov/buy-for-missouri)  
    **Benefits:**

    
* **Cost Savings:** Access to competitively bid contracts can result in significant cost reductions for participating entities.â€‹  
    
* **Efficiency:** Streamlined procurement processes reduce administrative burdens and expedite acquisitions.â€‹  
    
  **Participation:**  
    
* **Eligibility:** Local governments, political subdivisions, and quasi-public governmental bodies within Missouri.â€‹  
    
* **Process:** Interested entities can apply to join the Cooperative Procurement Program through the Missouri Office of Administration's Division of Purchasing.â€‹  
    
  ---

    
  **Recommendations for Scan2Plan:**  
    
* **Register on MissouriBUYS:** Ensure that Scan2Plan is registered in Missouri's eProcurement system to access and respond to state-level solicitations.â€‹  
    
* **Explore Cooperative Purchasing Opportunities:** Consider participating in cooperative purchasing ventures through the state's program to expand potential procurement opportunities.â€‹  
    
* **Utilize Available Resources:** Leverage training materials, vendor guides, and help desks provided by both state and municipal procurement offices to navigate the procurement processes effectively.â€‹  
    
  By following these steps and utilizing the resources provided, Scan2Plan can effectively engage with Missouri's procurement processes and explore potential opportunities within the state.

* **Register with the State's Materiel Division:** Ensure that Scan2Plan is registered as a vendor with Nebraska's Materiel Division to access and respond to state-level solicitations.â€‹[das.nebraska.gov](https://das.nebraska.gov/materiel/)  
    
* **Explore Municipal Opportunities:** Identify key municipalities that align with Scan2Plan's services and register on their procurement portals or monitor their official websites for bid opportunities.â€‹  
    
* **Utilize Available Resources:** Leverage training materials, vendor guides, and help desks provided by both state and municipal procurement offices to navigate the procurement processes effectively.â€‹  
    
  By following these steps and utilizing the resources provided, Scan2Plan can effectively engage with Nebraska's procurement processes and explore potential opportunities within the state.

  # **Nevada**

* **NevadaEPro**: [https://nevadaepro.com/bso/](https://nevadaepro.com/bso/)  
    
  Engaging with Nevada's procurement processes involves understanding both state-level systems and municipal platforms. Here's a comprehensive guide to assist you:  
    
  ---

  ## **1\. State-Level Procurement: NevadaEPro System**

  **Overview:**  
    
  The State of Nevada utilizes **NevadaEPro**, an electronic procurement system managed by the Nevada State Purchasing Division. This platform facilitates vendor registration, solicitation postings, electronic bidding, and contract management, ensuring transparency and efficiency in the state's procurement activities. â€‹[purchasing.nv.gov+6purchasing.nv.gov+6test.nevadaepro.com+6](https://purchasing.nv.gov/Vendors/Registration/)  
    
  **Access:**  
    
* **Website:** NevadaEPro  
    
  **Registration Process:**  
    
1. **Vendor Registration:**  
     
   * Visit the [NevadaEPro portal](https://nevadaepro.com/bso/).â€‹[nevadaepro.com+1test.nevadaepro.com+1](https://nevadaepro.com/bso/)  
       
   * Complete the registration form by providing necessary business information, including contact details and relevant documentation.â€‹  
       
   * Once registered, vendors can receive notifications of bid opportunities, submit proposals electronically, and manage their profiles.â€‹  
       
     **Bid Opportunities:**

     
* Current solicitations are posted on the NevadaEPro platform. Vendors can browse open bids, access solicitation documents, and submit responses electronically. â€‹[publicworks.nv.gov+5purchasing.nv.gov+5nevadaepro.com+5](https://purchasing.nv.gov/NevadaEPro/)  
    
  **Assistance:**  
    
* **NevadaEPro Help Desk:**  
    
  * **Phone:** (775) 684-0176â€‹[controller.nv.gov+1purchasing.nv.gov+1](https://controller.nv.gov/Vendor/VendorServices/)  
      
  * **Email:** [NevadaEPro@admin.nv.gov](mailto:NevadaEPro@admin.nv.gov)â€‹[purchasing.nv.gov+5controller.nv.gov+5purchasing.nv.gov+5](https://controller.nv.gov/Vendor/VendorServices/)

    ## **2\. Municipal Procurement Portals**

    **Nevada Government eMarketplace (NGEM):**  
    NGEM is a collaborative effort among local government entities in Nevada, providing a centralized platform for contractors and suppliers to receive requests for bids or proposals from participating entities at no charge. â€‹[lasvegasnevada.gov+1bcnv.org+1](https://www.lasvegasnevada.gov/Business/Purchasing/Purchasing-Resources/tab/1)

* **Website:** City of Las Vegas Purchasing  
    
  **City of Boulder City:**

* **Website:** Boulder City Bids, RFPs, and RFQs  
    
  **Other Municipalities:**  
    
  Various cities and counties in Nevada have established procurement portals or provide bid opportunities through their official websites. For a comprehensive list of municipal bid notices in Nevada, vendors can refer to [US Public Works \- Nevada Bid Notices](https://uspublicworks.com/nevada-bid-notices-cities-towns-and-municipalities/). â€‹[uspublicworks.com](https://uspublicworks.com/nevada-bid-notices-cities-towns-and-municipalities/)

  # **New Hampshire**

  #### **State-Level Procurement Systems**

  ##### **New Hampshire Department of Administrative Services \- Bureau of Purchase and Property**

* **NH Statewide Procurement Portal**:  
    
  * Website: [https://das.nh.gov/purchasing](https://das.nh.gov/purchasing)  
  * The central hub for state procurement, vendor registration, and bid opportunities.  
  * Hosts solicitations for all state agencies, boards, and commissions.


* **Vendor Registration and Bidder Information**:  
    
  * Vendors must register to access bid opportunities and submit proposals.  
  * Registration process includes providing business information and accepting the stateâ€™s procurement terms.  
  * Once registered, vendors receive bid notifications based on their selected categories.


* **NH Bureau of Purchase and Property â€“ Active Bids**:  
    
  * Website: [https://das.nh.gov/purchasing/bids\_posteddp.asp](https://das.nh.gov/purchasing/bids_posteddp.asp)  
  * Lists open and closed solicitations, including deadlines and document downloads.


* **NH Statewide Contracts**:  
    
  * Offers cooperative purchasing contracts available to local municipalities.  
      
  * Allows vendors to engage in long-term procurement agreements with the state.

    #### **Key Municipal Procurement Portals**

    ##### **City of Manchester**

* **Manchester Purchasing Division**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.manchesternh.gov/Departments/Purchasing](https://www.manchesternh.gov/Departments/Purchasing)  
      
  * Handles all city procurement, including construction, professional services, and goods.  
      
  * Vendors can register and bid electronically through the portal.

    ##### **City of Nashua**

* **Nashua Procurement Portal**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.nashuanh.gov/228/Purchasing](https://www.nashuanh.gov/228/Purchasing)  
      
  * Provides a vendor registration platform, bid postings, and procurement policies.  
      
  * Includes an online RFP submission system for vendors.

    ##### **City of Concord**

* **Concord Purchasing Division**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.concordnh.gov/656/Purchasing](https://www.concordnh.gov/656/Purchasing)  
      
  * Lists active bid opportunities and contracting procedures for city projects.  
      
  * Vendors must be pre-qualified for certain contracts, especially for public works.

    ##### **City of Portsmouth**

* **Portsmouth Procurement Office**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.cityofportsmouth.com/finance/purchasing-bids-rfps](https://www.cityofportsmouth.com/finance/purchasing-bids-rfps)  
      
  * Provides open solicitations and vendor registration forms.  
      
  * Publishes RFPs for city infrastructure and service contracts.

    #### **Cooperative Purchasing Programs**

    ##### **NH Purchasing Cooperative**

* A consortium of municipalities that pools procurement needs to obtain better pricing and contract terms.  
    
* Website: [https://www.nhmunicipal.org](https://www.nhmunicipal.org/)  
    
* Members include counties, cities, and school districts looking to save on bulk purchases.

  ##### **New England Governmental Purchasing Cooperative (NEGPC)**

* Multi-state cooperative including New Hampshire, offering cooperative contracts for municipal and state entities.  
    
* Allows vendors to supply goods and services to multiple New England states under one contract.  
    
* Website: [https://negpc.org](https://negpc.org/)

  #### **Vendor Registration Requirements**

* Most state and municipal procurement portals require:  
    
  * Business registration and tax ID.  
      
  * Insurance and bonding documentation (if applicable).  
      
  * Compliance with state procurement laws and bidding procedures.  
      
  * Electronic bid submission capability.

    #### **Summary**

    New Hampshireâ€™s procurement landscape includes a centralized state purchasing portal alongside active municipal procurement sites in major cities such as Manchester, Nashua, Concord, and Portsmouth. Vendors should register with both state and municipal systems to maximize procurement opportunities. Cooperative purchasing programs further streamline opportunities for vendors seeking multi-jurisdiction contracts. The state's focus on transparency and competitive bidding makes it an accessible market for procurement activities.

  * Complete separate registrations for municipal and county procurement systems.  
      
  * Provide business licensing, tax ID, and insurance documentation.  
      
  * Adhere to bid submission guidelines for electronic or paper-based proposals.

    #### **Summary**

    New Mexicoâ€™s procurement structure is highly organized with a centralized **eProNM** system for state-level contracts, complemented by robust municipal purchasing portals in major cities such as Albuquerque, Santa Fe, and Las Cruces. Cooperative purchasing agreements further expand vendor opportunities, making it essential for businesses to register with multiple procurement platforms to maximize opportunities. The stateâ€™s procurement policies emphasize transparency and competitive bidding, making it accessible for vendors across various industries.

    # **New York**

* **New York State Contract Reporter**: [https://www.nyscr.ny.gov/](https://www.nyscr.ny.gov/)â€‹[en.wikipedia.org](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_York_State_Register)

  **Comprehensive Guide to State and Municipal Procurement Portals**

  ### **New York \- Part 1: State-Level Procurement Systems**

  #### **New York State Office of General Services (OGS) \- Procurement Services**

* **New York Statewide eProcurement System (NYS Contract Reporter)**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.nyscr.ny.gov](https://www.nyscr.ny.gov/)  
  * The official procurement portal for all New York State agencies, authorities, and public benefit corporations.  
  * Vendors must register to access solicitation notices, contract opportunities, and RFPs.


* **Vendor Registration and Bidder Information**:  
    
  * Registration is required through the **NYS Contract System**.  
  * Allows vendors to receive bid notifications and submit electronic proposals.  
  * Provides access to state contract awards and procurement analytics.


* **Statewide Contracts and Cooperative Purchasing**:  
    
  * Website: [https://ogs.ny.gov/procurement](https://ogs.ny.gov/procurement)  
      
  * Lists active statewide contracts available for municipal and local government use.  
      
  * Includes term contracts and discretionary purchasing options for qualified vendors.

    #### **New York State Department of Transportation (NYSDOT) \- Procurement Division**

* **NYSDOT Procurement and Contracting Opportunities**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.dot.ny.gov/business](https://www.dot.ny.gov/business)  
      
  * Manages transportation-related contracts, construction projects, and consultant procurements.  
      
  * Vendors must register in the **New York State Vendor Responsibility System** for eligibility.

    #### **Empire State Development (ESD) \- MWBE & SDVOB Procurement Assistance**

* **Minority and Women-Owned Business Enterprises (MWBE) and Service-Disabled Veteran-Owned Businesses (SDVOB) Participation**:  
    
  * Website: [https://esd.ny.gov/mwbe](https://esd.ny.gov/mwbe)  
      
  * Facilitates procurement opportunities for MWBE and SDVOB-certified businesses.  
      
  * Maintains a directory of certified firms and provides access to government contracts.

    #### **New York State Thruway Authority (NYSTA) \- Procurement Services**

  * Website: [https://www.thruway.ny.gov/business/procurement](https://www.thruway.ny.gov/business/procurement)  
      
  * Manages contracts for infrastructure projects, maintenance services, and toll operations.  
      
  * Vendors can view solicitations and register for upcoming bids.

    #### **New York Power Authority (NYPA) \- Procurement Opportunities**

* **NYPA Supplier Portal**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.nypa.gov/procurement](https://www.nypa.gov/procurement)  
      
  * Facilitates procurement for energy projects, infrastructure improvements, and sustainability initiatives.  
      
  * Vendors can register and submit proposals electronically.

    #### **Vendor Registration Requirements**

* Businesses seeking to participate in New York State procurement must:  
    
  * Register with **NYS Contract Reporter** for state contracts.  
      
  * Complete the **Vendor Responsibility Questionnaire** for eligibility.  
      
  * Obtain MWBE or SDVOB certification for diversity-based procurement incentives.  
      
  * Provide required business licensing, tax ID, and insurance documentation.

    #### **Summary**

    ## New Yorkâ€™s state-level procurement system is one of the most comprehensive in the country, featuring a centralized **NYS Contract Reporter** for all state solicitations. Additional agencies, including NYSDOT, NYSTA, NYPA, and Empire State Development, provide specialized procurement opportunities for infrastructure, transportation, and economic development projects. Vendors should ensure registration across multiple platforms to maximize contract opportunities.
