* Facilitates cooperative purchasing for public school districts statewide.  
    
* Offers bulk purchasing agreements for technology, facilities, and educational supplies.

  #### **US Communities Government Purchasing Alliance**

* Website: [https://www.omniapartners.com/publicsector](https://www.omniapartners.com/publicsector)  
    
* Multi-state cooperative purchasing group used by North Carolina municipalities.  
    
* Offers cost savings through volume purchasing agreements.

  #### **National IPA (NIPA) \- Cooperative Purchasing Program**

* Website: [https://www.nationalipa.org](https://www.nationalipa.org/)  
    
* Provides cooperative contracts for government agencies, including those in North Carolina.

  #### **Summary**

  Cooperative purchasing programs allow North Carolina vendors to engage in multiple agency contracts under **pre-negotiated agreements**. Vendors should consider participating in **NCSPA, NCSBA, and national cooperative groups** like **Omnia Partners and NIPA** to expand procurement opportunities statewide.

    #### **Vendor Registration Requirements**

* Businesses seeking to participate in North Dakota state procurement must:  
    
  * Register with **ND OMBâ€™s State Procurement Portal** for state contracts.  
      
  * Provide business licensing, tax ID, and insurance documentation.  
      
  * Adhere to bid submission guidelines for electronic or paper-based proposals.

    #### **Summary**

    ## North Dakotaâ€™s state procurement system is centralized under the **ND OMB Procurement Portal**, which facilitates bid access for vendors statewide. Agencies such as **NDDOT, NDUS, and NDDHHS** offer additional specialized procurement opportunities. Vendors should register with multiple platforms to maximize contract eligibility.

  * Website: [https://www.dhs.pa.gov/providers/Procurement](https://www.dhs.pa.gov/providers/Procurement)  
      
  * Manages procurement for public health programs, social services, and state healthcare facilities.  
      
  * Vendors must comply with state health procurement guidelines.

    #### **Vendor Registration Requirements**

* Businesses seeking to participate in Pennsylvania state procurement must:  
    
  * Register with **Pennsylvania eMarketplace** for state contracts.  
      
  * Obtain **SDB or VBE certification** if applicable.  
      
  * Provide business licensing, tax ID, and insurance documentation.  
      
  * Adhere to bid submission guidelines for electronic or paper-based proposals.

    #### **Summary**

    ## Pennsylvaniaâ€™s state procurement system is centralized under the **Pennsylvania eMarketplace** platform, which facilitates bid access for vendors statewide. Agencies such as **PennDOT, PASSHE, DHS, and the Small Diverse Business Assistance Program** offer additional specialized procurement opportunities. Vendors should register with multiple platforms to maximize contract eligibility.

    ### **South Dakota \- Part 3: Cooperative Purchasing Programs and Additional Procurement Resources**

    #### **South Dakota Statewide Procurement Program (SDSPP)**

* Website: [https://boa.sd.gov/purchasing/contracts.aspx](https://boa.sd.gov/purchasing/contracts.aspx)  
    
* Supports cooperative purchasing efforts across state agencies and municipalities.  
    
* Provides pre-negotiated contracts for vendors serving multiple government entities.

  #### **South Dakota Municipal League (SDML) Purchasing Program**

* Website: [https://www.sdmunicipalleague.org](https://www.sdmunicipalleague.org/)  
    
* Facilitates cooperative purchasing for municipal governments statewide.  
    
* Offers bulk purchasing agreements for municipal projects and services.

  #### **NASPO ValuePoint \- National Cooperative Procurement Group**

* Website: [https://www.naspovaluepoint.org](https://www.naspovaluepoint.org/)  
    
* Multi-state cooperative purchasing group used by South Dakota municipalities.  
    
* Offers cost savings through volume purchasing agreements.

  #### **National Cooperative Purchasing Alliance (NCPA)**

* Website: [https://www.ncpa.us](https://www.ncpa.us/)  
    
* Provides cooperative contracts for government agencies, including those in South Dakota.

  #### **Summary**

  Cooperative purchasing programs allow South Dakota vendors to engage in multiple agency contracts under **pre-negotiated agreements**. Vendors should consider participating in **SDSPP, SDML, and national cooperative groups** like **NASPO ValuePoint and NCPA** to expand procurement opportunities statewide.

  * The official procurement system for all Tennessee state agencies, higher education institutions, and local governments.  
  * Vendors must register to access solicitation notices, contract opportunities, and RFPs.


* **Vendor Registration and Bidder Information**:  
    
  * Registration is required through **Edison**.  
  * Allows vendors to receive bid notifications and submit electronic proposals.  
  * Provides access to state contract awards and procurement analytics.


* **Statewide Contracts and Cooperative Purchasing**:

  * Website: [https://www.tn.gov/health/doing-business-with-tdoh.html](https://www.tn.gov/health/doing-business-with-tdoh.html)  
      
  * Manages procurement for public health programs, social services, and state healthcare facilities.  
      
  * Vendors must comply with state health procurement guidelines.

    #### **Vendor Registration Requirements**

* Businesses seeking to participate in Tennessee state procurement must:  
    
  * Register with **Edison** for state contracts.  
      
  * Obtain **small and minority business certification** if applicable.  
      
  * Provide business licensing, tax ID, and insurance documentation.  
      
  * Adhere to bid submission guidelines for electronic or paper-based proposals.

    #### **Summary**

    ## Tennesseeâ€™s state procurement system is centralized under the **Edison** platform, which facilitates bid access for vendors statewide. Agencies such as **TDOT, Tennessee Board of Regents, TDOH, and the Governorâ€™s Office of Diversity Business Enterprise** offer additional specialized procurement opportunities. Vendors should register with multiple platforms to maximize contract eligibility.

  ### **Virginia \- Part 1: State-Level Procurement Systems**

* **eVA \- Virginiaâ€™s Statewide eProcurement System**:  
    
  * Website: [https://eva.virginia.gov](https://eva.virginia.gov/)  
  * The official procurement system for all Virginia state agencies, higher education institutions, and local governments.  
  * Vendors must register to access solicitation notices, contract opportunities, and RFPs.


* **Vendor Registration and Bidder Information**:  
    
  * Registration is required through **eVA**.  
  * Allows vendors to receive bid notifications and submit electronic proposals.  
  * Provides access to state contract awards and procurement analytics.


* **Statewide Contracts and Cooperative Purchasing**:  
    
  * Website: [https://dgs.virginia.gov/procurement](https://dgs.virginia.gov/procurement)  
      
  * Lists active statewide contracts available for municipal and local government use.  
      
  * Includes term contracts and discretionary purchasing options for qualified vendors.

  * Vendors must register with **eVA** for eligibility.

    #### **Virginia Department of Small Business & Supplier Diversity (SBSD)**

  * Website: [https://www.sbsd.virginia.gov](https://www.sbsd.virginia.gov/)  
      
  * Facilitates procurement opportunities for small and minority-owned businesses.  
      
  * Provides training and networking opportunities for vendors.

  * Website: [https://www.vdh.virginia.gov/administration/procurement/](https://www.vdh.virginia.gov/administration/procurement/)  
      
  * Manages procurement for public health programs, social services, and state healthcare facilities.  
      
  * Vendors must comply with state health procurement guidelines.

    #### **Vendor Registration Requirements**

* Businesses seeking to participate in Virginia state procurement must:  
    
  * Register with **eVA** for state contracts.  
      
  * Obtain **SWaM certification** if applicable.  
      
  * Provide business licensing, tax ID, and insurance documentation.  
      
  * Adhere to bid submission guidelines for electronic or paper-based proposals.

    #### **Summary**

    ## Virginiaâ€™s state procurement system is centralized under the **eVA** platform, which facilitates bid access for vendors statewide. Agencies such as **VDOT, Virginia Higher Education Procurement, VDH, and SBSD** offer additional specialized procurement opportunities. Vendors should register with multiple platforms to maximize contract eligibility.

    ## Wisconsinâ€™s municipal procurement landscape includes independent purchasing portals for major cities such as **Milwaukee, Madison, Green Bay, Kenosha, and Racine**. Each city manages its own procurement system, requiring separate vendor registration. Vendors should register with each city to maximize access to local government contracts.

    ### **Wisconsin \- Part 3: Cooperative Purchasing Programs and Additional Procurement Resources**

    #### **Wisconsin Statewide Cooperative Purchasing Program (WSCPP)**

* Website: [https://doa.wi.gov/Pages/StateEmployees/Cooperative-Purchasing.aspx](https://doa.wi.gov/Pages/StateEmployees/Cooperative-Purchasing.aspx)  
    
* Supports cooperative purchasing efforts across state agencies and municipalities.  
    
* Provides pre-negotiated contracts for vendors serving multiple government entities.

  #### **Wisconsin Association of School Boards (WASB) Purchasing Program**

* Website: [https://www.wasb.org](https://www.wasb.org/)  
    
* Facilitates cooperative purchasing for school districts statewide.  
    
* Offers bulk purchasing agreements for technology, facilities, and educational supplies.

  #### **NASPO ValuePoint \- National Cooperative Procurement Group**

* Website: [https://www.naspovaluepoint.org](https://www.naspovaluepoint.org/)  
    
* Multi-state cooperative purchasing group used by Wisconsin municipalities.  
    
* Offers cost savings through volume purchasing agreements.

  #### **National Cooperative Purchasing Alliance (NCPA)**

* Website: [https://www.ncpa.us](https://www.ncpa.us/)  
    
* Provides cooperative contracts for government agencies, including those in Wisconsin.

  #### **Summary**

  Cooperative purchasing programs allow Wisconsin vendors to engage in multiple agency contracts under **pre-negotiated agreements**. Vendors should consider participating in **WSCPP, WASB, and national cooperative groups** like **NASPO ValuePoint and NCPA** to expand procurement opportunities statewide.

  # **Wyoming**

* **Wyoming State Procurement**: [http://ai.wyo.gov/general-services/procurement-sectionâ€‹](http://ai.wyo.gov/general-services/procurement-sectionâ€‹)  
    
  **Comprehensive Guide to State and Municipal Procurement Portals**

  ### **Wyoming \- Part 1: State-Level Procurement Systems**

  #### **Wyoming State Procurement Office \- Department of Administration & Information**

* **Public Purchase \- Statewide eProcurement System**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.publicpurchase.com](https://www.publicpurchase.com/)  
  * The official procurement system for all Wyoming state agencies, higher education institutions, and local governments.  
  * Vendors must register to access solicitation notices, contract opportunities, and RFPs.


* **Vendor Registration and Bidder Information**:  
    
  * Registration is required through **Public Purchase**.  
  * Allows vendors to receive bid notifications and submit electronic proposals.  
  * Provides access to state contract awards and procurement analytics.


* **Statewide Contracts and Cooperative Purchasing**:  
    
  * Website: [https://ai.wyo.gov/divisions/general-services/purchasing](https://ai.wyo.gov/divisions/general-services/purchasing)  
      
  * Lists active statewide contracts available for municipal and local government use.  
      
  * Includes term contracts and discretionary purchasing options for qualified vendors.

    #### **Wyoming Department of Transportation (WYDOT) \- Procurement Division**

* **WYDOT Procurement and Contracting Opportunities**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.dot.state.wy.us/home/business\_with\_wydot.html](https://www.dot.state.wy.us/home/business_with_wydot.html)  
      
  * Manages transportation-related contracts, construction projects, and consultant procurements.  
      
  * Vendors must register with **Public Purchase** for eligibility.

    #### **Wyoming Small and Minority Business Assistance Programs**

* **Wyoming Small Business Development Center (SBDC) & Disadvantaged Business Enterprise (DBE) Program**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.wyomingsbdc.org](https://www.wyomingsbdc.org/)  
      
  * Facilitates procurement opportunities for small and minority-owned businesses.  
      
  * Provides training and networking opportunities for vendors.

    #### **University of Wyoming \- Higher Education Procurement**

* **University of Wyoming Procurement Opportunities**:  
    
  * Website: [https://www.uwyo.edu/procurement](https://www.uwyo.edu/procurement)  
      
  * Manages procurement for Wyomingâ€™s only public university.  
      
  * Vendors can access bid opportunities for university projects.

    #### **Wyoming Department of Health (WDH) \- Procurement Services**

* **WDH Vendor Registration and Procurement**:  
    
  * Website: [https://health.wyo.gov/admin/contracting/](https://health.wyo.gov/admin/contracting/)  
      
  * Manages procurement for public health programs, social services, and state healthcare facilities.  
      
  * Vendors must comply with state health procurement guidelines.

    #### **Vendor Registration Requirements**

* Businesses seeking to participate in Wyoming state procurement must:  
    
  * Register with **Public Purchase** for state contracts.  
      
  * Obtain **DBE certification** if applicable.  
      
  * Provide business licensing, tax ID, and insurance documentation.  
      
  * Adhere to bid submission guidelines for electronic or paper-based proposals.

    #### **Summary**

    ## Wyomingâ€™s state procurement system is centralized under the **Public Purchase** platform, which facilitates bid access for vendors statewide. Agencies such as **WYDOT, University of Wyoming, WDH, and SBDC** offer additional specialized procurement opportunities. Vendors should register with multiple platforms to maximize contract eligibility.
